# Dataiku Docs — thirdparty

## [thirdparty/solutions]

# Dataiku Solutions

Several Dataiku Solutions use and distribute third party software under the following licenses. To the extent that Dataiku Solutions leverage the technology of the Dataiku DSS, the list of OSS components used and [distributed by DSS](<dss.html>) is also applicable.

Note

Some of the mentioned third-party Python packages are installed in a code environment by the user, and not directly distributed within the Dataiku Solution.
